    <section class="core-section-container

<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Mplus is a European leader in business process and technology outsourcing (BPTO). It operates as part of the BOSQAR INVEST group, serving as its BPTO vertical, which includes the parent company, M Plus Croatia d.o.o, along with its subsidiaries.

Mplus successfully integrates the dynamic industries of contact centers, information technology, and employment services to address global challenges in customer support. Through its innovative business model, Mplus has built a diverse portfolio of clients, including leading European and global telecommunications, financial, technology, energy, logistics, and consumer goods companies.

With operational centers across 42 sites in 13 countries, the Mplus community comprises over 12,800 employees who deliver top-notch customer experiences in over 32 languages.

In addition to its presence in Croatia, Mplus operates in markets including Bosnia and Herzegovina, Georgia, Germany, Hungary, Romania, Serbia, Slovakia, Slovenia, Spain, Turkey, the UK, and the USA.

Mplus has an in-house technology division, which brings together the tech companies within the BPTO group. Their wide range of products, services, and consulting solutions is carefully designed to transform how companies interact with their customers and manage their processes, offering cutting-edge tools to enhance customer experience, optimize operations, and embrace digital transformation.
          </p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary"> 
🌟 Celebrating 25 Years of People-Centered Innovation at Mplus Türkiye!
 
<a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/mplusturkiye?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mplus Türkiye</a> recently marked its 25th anniversary with a special event, celebrating a quarter-century of achievements and sharing strategic goals for the future.

The celebration began with a warm welcome from <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/luka-oreskovic-31719733?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Luka Oreskovic</a>, Chairman of the Advisory Board of Mplus, followed by inspiring words from <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/cemile-banu-hizli?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Cemile Banu Hizli</a>, CEO of Mplus Türkiye &amp; MENA.

“Our corporate culture, built on trust and transparency, has not only fueled our growth but also become a transformation story that inspires the industry,” Banu said.

The event brought together senior leadership from across the group, including <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/darko-horvat-81a771190?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Darko Horvat</a>, <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/tomislav-glava%C5%A1-15812492?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Tomislav Glavaš</a>, and <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/vanja-vlak-15430a40?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Vanja Vlak</a>, whose presence underscored the strong partnership and shared vision driving the future of Mplus and the broader <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/bosqar-invest?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>BOSQAR INVEST</a> group.

As Banu Hızlı emphasized: 

“As a team, we have always prioritized our values, maintaining a collaborative and customer-focused spirit. We choose to do what is right, not what is easy, with love and respect. Most importantly, in a complex and rapidly changing world, keeping promises, giving our best, and remaining fair, honest, and transparent has always guided us.”

Here’s to the next 25 years of creating meaningful connections and transforming customer experiences! 🎉

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🏆We came back from Rovinj with four HR awards!

Mplus has been recognized as a Top Workplace on a group level (12,500+ employees) and received the Best of the Best Award in several Mplus companies in the region: <a class="link" href="https://si.linkedin.com/company/mpluslovenia?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mplus Slovenia</a>, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/mplusbosniaherzegovina?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mplus Bosnia &amp; Herzegovina</a>, and <a class="link" href="https://rs.linkedin.com/company/mpluserbia?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mplus Serbia</a>!

These awards, presented by <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/luppa-app?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Luppa</a>, were announced during this year’s <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/hr-weekend?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>HR.WEEKEND</a>, a perfect setting to celebrate our shared achievements.

Here’s what makes it special:

•	Top Workplace goes to companies scoring at least 15% above industry benchmarks in engagement, satisfaction, eNPS, and Luppa’s 12 dimensions.
•	Best of the Best celebrates organizations that exceed both benchmarks by 25% or more and rank among the top three in their market and size category - true leaders in creating exceptional workplaces.

"These awards are more than recognition - they’re a reflection of real feedback and the daily effort of our people: management, HR, and employees alike. Thanks to Luppa, we now have deeper insights than ever to turn feedback into meaningful action. At Mplus, people inspire people, and that’s what these awards celebrate!", <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/bruna-kostelac-ko%C5%A1ir-9b31582?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Bruna Kostelac Košir</a>, Chief People Officer at Mplus said.

A huge thank you to everyone who contributes to making Mplus a great place to work!

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">At this year’s <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/weekend-media-festival?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Weekend Media Festival</a> in Rovinj, Mplus's Chief People Officer, <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/bruna-kostelac-ko%C5%A1ir-9b31582?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Bruna Kostelac Košir</a>, moderated the panel, "It’s a Kind of Magic! When HR Drives the ESG Agenda". She was joined on stage by <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/lucia-ana-tomi%C4%87-57b0869?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Lucia Ana Tomić</a> (<a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/wiener-osiguranje-vienna-insurance-group-d.d.?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Wiener osiguranje Vienna Insurance Group d.d.</a> ) and <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/hana-hrpka-74908855?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Hana Hrpka</a> (<a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/hrabri-telefon?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Hrabri telefon (Brave phone)</a>).

The discussion highlighted a crucial point: people bring ESG strategies to life. Panelists agreed that HR’s role is expanding – proactive leadership is essential. ESG strategies can only succeed when HR steps up and takes responsibility, rather than playing the “not my job” card.

As Bruna concluded: “If you want to be truly strategic, start with your core business – identify what you do best and which NGO you can support most effectively. That’s how real partnerships are built.”

For more insights from the panel, see the full announcement here: <a class="link" href="http://tinyurl.com/5n8wduj9?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>tinyurl.com/5n8wduj9</a>

          gap-0.125 h-[425px] babybear:h-[360px]" data-test-id="feed-images-content">
              <li class="bg-color-background-container-tint text-[0px]
                  col-span-full 
                  
                  
                  " data-test-id="feed-images-content__list-item" data-position="0" style>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">ESG has made its way to boardroom agendas. But what happens when HR turns strategies into real impact?

Mplus's Chief People Officer, <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/bruna-kostelac-ko%C5%A1ir-9b31582?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Bruna Kostelac Košir</a>, will take on that very question as the moderator of a panel bringing together two powerful perspectives:

🔸 <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/lucia-ana-tomi%C4%87-57b0869?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Lucia Ana Tomić</a> – Head of HR and Regulatory Affairs, <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/wiener-osiguranje-vienna-insurance-group-d.d.?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Wiener osiguranje Vienna Insurance Group d.d.</a>
🔸 <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/hana-hrpka-74908855?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Hana Hrpka</a> – Executive Director &amp; President, <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/hrabri-telefon?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Hrabri telefon (Brave phone)</a>

The conversation will cut through theory and dive into:

✨ how talent and culture can push and co-create ESG strategy,
✨ how HR can measure the impact of ESG,
✨ and what it looks like when change reaches beyond business and into community.

Not a buzzword session. A real look at what happens when HR leads on ESG.

👉 Don’t miss it. See you at the <a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/company/hr-weekend?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>HR.WEEKEND</a> in Rovinj!

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fhrweekend&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#HRweekend</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fweekendsvihweekenda&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#WeekendSvihWeekenda</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🚀 Mplus is a finalist at The 2025 A.I. Awards!

We’re proud to share that Mplus has been named a finalist in two categories at this year’s A.I. Awards, operated by <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/cloud-saas-awards?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>The Cloud Awards</a> program:

🛰 Best Use of AI in Telecoms / Unified Communications / Conferencing

🚚 Best Use of AI in Transportation &amp; Logistics

The A.I. Awards celebrate global leaders driving innovation in artificial intelligence across sectors such as telecoms, retail, law, entertainment, and healthcare. This year, competition is tougher than ever, with entries spanning North America, Europe, the Middle East, and APAC.

“Being named a finalist in two categories is a great endorsement of our hard work in delivering exceptional value through AI to our customers and partners. We look forward to the final results and wish all fellow finalists the best of luck,” <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/kodaskurzewski?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Koda Skurzewski (Sker - je - ski ), OMCP</a>, Mplus Board Member and Chief Commercial Officer, said.

Winners will be revealed on October 13. 🏆

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Exciting news! Mplus has been shortlisted for nine categories at the prestigious 2025 A.I. Awards, a global program celebrating the brightest innovations in artificial intelligence.

The group has been shortlisted in the following categories:

 🔹 Best Use of AI in Transportation &amp; Logistics
 🔹 AI Deployment of the Year
 🔹 Best AI-driven Automation Solution
 🔹 Best Use of AI in Natural Language Processing (NLP) and Translation
 🔹 Most Advanced AI Environment
 🔹 Best Use of AI in Customer Service
 🔹 Best Use of AI in Telecoms / Unified Communications / Conferencing
 🔹 Best Use of AI in Retail &amp; eCommerce
 🔹 Best Use of AI-driven Personalization

The recognition places Mplus alongside leading international technology players such as IBM, Cognizant, Genesys, Capital One, DeepL, Bloomreach, and Talkdesk. 

“Mplus’s multi-category recognition at the A.I. Awards is a testament to our commitment to delivering practical, impactful AI solutions that enhance customer experiences and operational efficiency across industries,” said <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/kodaskurzewski?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Koda Skurzewski (Sker - je - ski ), OMCP</a>, Board Member and Chief Commercial Officer at Mplus. 

“To be recognized alongside some of the world’s most influential AI innovators is both an honor and a motivator as we continue to invest in next-generation technologies,” she added.

Winners will be announced in October 2025, with honorees selected from across the US, Canada, Europe, Asia, and Australia.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🏆 We won Gold!

Mplus has received the Gold award at the 2025 <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/brandonhallgroup?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Brandon Hall Group</a>™ HCM Excellence Awards® in the Leadership Development category for our Global Frontline Leaders Development Program 2.0, delivered through Mplus Academy.

This program is more than a training initiative – it empowers our team leaders to navigate challenges, foster innovation, and drive success across our global organization. 

<a class="link" href="https://hr.linkedin.com/in/bruna-kostelac-ko%C5%A1ir-9b31582?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Bruna Kostelac Košir</a>, Chief People Officer at Mplus, said: "This Gold award reflects our team’s dedication, creativity, and commitment to developing future-ready leaders. I want to personally thank everyone involved – your hard work made this achievement possible!"

<a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/kaaniseder?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Kaan İlker İşeder, MBA, PCC</a>, Group Head of Talent Development and Professional Executive Coach, added: "We are incredibly proud of this program and delighted to bring such a prestigious award to Mplus. Effective leadership is vital to our organization’s success."

For the full press release and more details about the program, read here: <a class="link" href="http://bit.ly/3HEV96b?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>bit.ly/3HEV96b</a>

Designed with <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/school/kocuniversity/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Koç University</a>’s bespoke development methodology – ranked #1 in Türkiye and #38 globally in the Financial Times 2025 list – it’s a testament to our belief in developing leaders who make a real impact.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">
As part of the first Mplus Culture Week, employees across nine countries took part in the Move &amp; Groove Challenge, a global step competition promoting wellness, motivation, and team spirit. 
 
Over just five days, participants achieved incredible results: 

14,957,032 steps – covering 11,218 km, nearly a quarter of Earth’s circumference 🌍 
 
54,787 steps per participant on average – roughly a marathon 🏃♀ 
 
Team Winner: 🇸🇮 Slovenia – 92,327 steps ⌚ 
 
Individual Winner: 🇷🇸 Serbia – 330,268 steps 🏆 – close to the distance from Zagreb to Madrid! 
 
The Move &amp; Groove Challenge proved that every step counts – and when we move together, we can achieve amazing things. 💪👟 
 
To find out more about Mplus Culture Week and all the exciting activities that took place, visit <a class="link" href="http://bit.ly/45lppvW?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>http://bit.ly/45lppvW</a>
